beginSubroutine: s32'CmnCutSceneDamage_Kakusei'
  ifOpponentCharacterMain: s16'pot'
  if: Mem(Tmp)
    debugLogForScript: s32'pot', 0, 0
  endIf: 
  ifOpponentCharacterMain: s16'fau'
  if: Mem(Tmp)
    debugLogForScript: s32'fau', 0, 0
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(FuncArg0), Val(19)
      debugLogForScript: s32'20', 0, 0
      storeValue: Mem(ActReg7), Val(0)
      findState: s32'cmn_AfroObj', 11, 2, 52
      isObjectActive: (STACK7)
      if: Mem(Tmp)
        runOnObject: (STACK7)
          setObjectWidth: 800
          setObjectHeight: 500
          setObjectDepth: 800
        endRunOnObject: 
      endIf: 
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(FuncArg0), Val(20)
      debugLogForScript: s32'160', 0, 0
      isObjectActive: (STACK7)
      if: Mem(Tmp)
        runOnObject: (STACK7)
          setObjectWidth: 1000
          setObjectHeight: 1200
          setObjectDepth: 1000
        endRunOnObject: 
      endIf: 
    endIf: 
  endIf: 
endSubroutine:

beginState: s32'CmnActStand'
  checkLastStateName: s32'CmnActFWalk'
  gotoLabelIf: s32'FWalk', Mem(Tmp)
  checkLastStateName: s32'CmnActBWalk'
  gotoLabelIf: s32'BWalk', Mem(Tmp)
  checkLastStateName: s32'CmnActBDash'
  gotoLabelIf: s32'BDash', Mem(Tmp)
  checkLastStateName: s32'CmnActBurst'
  gotoLabelIf: s32'Burst_Hajikare', Mem(Tmp)
  checkLastStateName: s32'CmnActHajikareAir'
  gotoLabelIf: s32'Burst_Hajikare', Mem(Tmp)
  checkLastStateName: s32'CmnActLandingStiff'
  gotoLabelIf: s32'LandingStiff', Mem(Tmp)
  beginLabel: s32'loop'
  sprite: s32'ven000_00', 8
  sprite: s32'ven000_01', 8
  sprite: s32'ven000_02', 8
  sprite: s32'ven000_03', 8
  sprite: s32'ven000_04', 8

  sprite: s32'ven000_11', 8
  endLabel: 
  gotoIfOperation: s32'loop', (PERCENT), Val(80), Val(100)
  gotoLabelIfNot: s32'loop', Mem(IsReactionReady)
  storeValue: Mem(ReactionWait), Val(600)
  sprite: s32'ven001_00', 5

      endIf:

beginSubroutine: s32'VEN_Special_05_Check'
  checkCurrentStateEntryName: s32'VEN_Special_05_S'
  if: Mem(Tmp)
    storeValue: Mem(ActReg0), Val(1)
  endIf: 
  checkCurrentStateEntryName: s32'VEN_Special_05_HS'
  if: Mem(Tmp)
    storeValue: Mem(ActReg0), Val(2)
  endIf: 
  upon: (NO_STOP_IDLING)
    checkInput: (INPUT_HOLD_P)
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg0), Val(1)
      checkInput: (INPUT_HOLD_S)
    endIf: 
    else: 
      ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg0), Val(2)
        checkInput: (INPUT_HOLD_H)
      endIf: 
    endElse: 
    if: Mem(Tmp)
      storeValue: Mem(ActReg1), Val(1)
    endIf: 
    else: 
      storeValue: Mem(ActReg1), Val(0)
      clearRegisteredUponCode: (NO_STOP_IDLING)
    endElse: 
  endUpon: 
  upon: (IDLING)
    ifNot: Mem(ActReg1)
      if: Mem(ActReg2)
        clearRegisteredUponCode: (IDLING)
        gotoLabelRequests: s32'hold_off'
      endIf: 
    endIf: 
  endUpon: 
endSubroutine:
